***grammaticaal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grammaticaal.html>grammaticaal</a> (64902)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:ultimately.html>Ultimately</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">grammaticālis</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grammatica.html>grammatica</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aal</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a> (69786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Genericization <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Granola" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Granola"><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>Granola</a></a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:name.html>name</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>an</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:early.html>early</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brand.html>brand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> cereal, <a href = vnd.unilang:itself.html>itself</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> variation <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Granula" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Granula">Granula</a></i>, invented <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Caleb_Jackson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:James Caleb Jackson"><a href = vnd.unilang:james.html>James</a> Caleb Jackson</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> 1863. <i>Granula</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> named <a href = vnd.unilang:after.html>after</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <span class="Latn" lang="en">granules</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Graham_flour" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Graham flour"><a href = vnd.unilang:graham.html>Graham</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:flour.html>flour</a></a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:main.html>main</a> ingredient<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></strong> (<i>countable <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">granolas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:breakfast.html>breakfast</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:snack.html>snack</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:food.html>food</a> consisting <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:loose.html>loose</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:crispy.html>crispy</a> pellets <a href = vnd.unilang:made.html>made</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nuts.html>nuts</a>, rolled <a href = vnd.unilang:oats.html>oats</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:honey.html>honey</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:other.html>other</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:natural.html>natural</a> ingredients.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:more.html>more</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:most.html>most</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:granola.html>granola</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gras.html>gras</a> (2942)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gras.html>gras</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:gras.html>gras</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grasą</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰreh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grow.html>grow</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***graver.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:graver.html>graver</a> (37125)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">grāvere</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:graven.html>graven</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijpen.html>grepe</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gripi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:grasp.html>grasp</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:clutch.html>clutch</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gripiz</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:variant.html>variant</a> nominative singular <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> preserved <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begrip.html>begrip</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijpen.html>grepe</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*grēpa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:handle.html>handle</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:grip.html>grip</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*graipō</i>.
</p>
